 




    High Street Conversion from One-Way to
              Two-Way Operations

     Appendix C - Lane Striping and Signage with the Proposed
                            Conversion




                                                                 
 



Appendix C: Lane Striping and Signage with the Proposed
Conversion
This section describes lane striping and signage modifications at the intersections and parking
considerations along High Street with the proposed conversion. The improvements are
discussed beginning at the intersection of High Street/Channing Avenue, up to the intersection
of High Street/Lytton Avenue.

One-way to Two-Way Operations between Channing Avenue and Forest Avenue

High Street/ Channing Avenue Intersection
   · Modify lane striping at the intersection to conform to two-way operations along High
       Street.
   · For the proposed northbound approach on High Street, remove the "Do Not Enter" signs
       posted along both sides of High Street and also remove the "right-turn only" sign painted
       on the pavement.
   · For the southbound approach on High Street, remove the sign "Left Lane Must Turn
       Left" and also remove the "Left-Turn" arrow painted on the pavement.
   · For the eastbound approach on Channing Avenue, remove the "No left-turn" sign and
       also the "One-Way" sign along High Street. Also modify lane striping on the eastbound
       lanes on Channing to indicate that vehicles can turn left onto High Street.

High Street ­ between Channing Avenue and Homer Avenue

    ·   Remove all signage at the driveways that indicate High Street as a one-way street.
    ·   At the 800 High Street parking garage driveway, remove the "one-way" sign along High
        Street.
    ·   At the Whole Foods parking lot driveway on High Street, remove the left-turn arrow
        painted on the driveway and also remove the "No Right-turn" sign.

High Street/ Homer Avenue Intersection

    ·   For the proposed northbound traffic on High Street approaching Homer Avenue, put up a
        "one-way" sign along Homer and a "No right-turn" sign along Homer to indicate Homer
        Avenue as a one-way street in the westbound direction.
    ·   For the westbound traffic on Homer Avenue approaching High Street, remove the "one-
        way" sign along High Street.

High Street ­ between Homer Avenue and Forest Avenue

    ·   The City should consider removing the first parking stall on the east side of High Street,
        to the immediate north of Homer Avenue to provide adequate sight distance and turning
        radius for vehicles on Homer Avenue to turn right onto High Street.

High Street/ Forest Avenue Intersection

    ·   With the proposed conversion, modify lane striping at the intersection to conform to two-
        way operations along High Street for the northbound approach on High Street. This
        intersection will go from a 3-way stop to a 4-way stop.


                                                                                                   
 


    ·   For the proposed northbound approach on High Street, install a stop-sign and paint
        "STOP" in the northbound travel lane on High Street approaching Forest Avenue.
        Pavement markings in the northbound travel lane approaching High Street should
        consist of shared left-right arrows indicating that vehicles can either turn left or right onto
        Forest Avenue. Also install "Do Not Enter" signs on both sides of High Street, facing the
        northbound approaching traffic.
    ·   For the southbound approach on High Street, the inner travel lane on the east should be
        striped as a left-turn lane with a sign indicating that vehicles in this lane must turn left.
    ·   It is recommended that the stop line on the westbound approach on Forest Avenue be
        offset back by at least 8 feet to provide adequate room for opposing left-turns on High
        Street.

Extension to Hamilton Avenue
The following lane striping improvements and signage modifications along High Street would
need to be implemented with the extension of the two-way conversion by an additional block up
to Hamilton Avenue:

High Street/ Forest Avenue Intersection

    ·   With the proposed conversion, modify lane striping at the intersection to conform to two-
        way operations along High Street. This intersection will go from a 3-way stop to a 4-way
        stop.
    ·   For the proposed northbound approach, install a stop-sign and paint "STOP" in the
        northbound travel lane on High Street approaching Forest Avenue.
    ·   For the westbound approach on Forest Avenue, remove the "No right-turn" sign and also
        the "one-way" sign along High Street. It is recommended that the stop line on the
        westbound approach on Forest Avenue be offset back by at least 8 feet to provide
        adequate room for opposing left-turns on High Street.
    ·   For the eastbound approach on Forest Avenue, remove the "one-way" sign along High
        Street and the "No left-turn" sign.

High Street ­ between Forest Avenue and Hamilton Avenue

    ·   Remove all "one-way" signs along High Street.

High Street/Hamilton Avenue Intersection

    ·   Remove lane striping on the southbound travel lanes on High Street in order to conform
        to two-way operations on High Street.
    ·   Pavement markings in the northbound travel lane approaching High Street should
        consist of shared left-right arrows indicating that vehicles can either turn left or right onto
        Hamilton Avenue. Also install "Do Not Enter" signs on both sides of High Street, facing
        the northbound approaching traffic.
    ·   For the southbound approach on High Street, the inner travel lane on the east should be
        striped as a left-turn lane with a sign indicating that vehicles in this lane must turn left.
